NAS, DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA'I MCHOD PA BYA'O, ,BZHI PO 'DI DAG NI
LHAG PA'I SEMS BSKYED PA STE, BZHI NI SEMS CAN BSDU BA DANG, SMIN
PAR BYA BA DANG, DGE BA'I RTZA BA BSAGS PA DANG,

CHOS RTOGS PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR SEMS BSKYED PA'O, ,SEMS BSKYED PA
BRAG CA LTA BU BZHI NI SLONG BA LA KHONG KHRO BA MED PA DANG, LOG
PAR ZHUGS PA LA SNYING RJE BA DANG, SHES RAB LAS MA NYAMS PA
DANG, RTZOL BA NYAMS 'OG TU CHUD PA'I SEMS SO, ,SEMS BSKYED

PA MNGON PAR 'PHAGS PA BZHI NI TSUL KHRIMS DANG, THOS PA DANG,
BYAMS PA DANG, SNYING RJE MNGON PAR 'PHAGS PA'O, ,SEMS BSKYED PA
RDO RJE LTA BU BZHI NI, BSAM PA DANG, MDZA' BA DANG, NAN TAN
DANG, THEG PA CHEN PO LAS MI PHYED PA'O, ,SEMS BSKYED PA RNYED

DKA' BA BZHI NI, NYON MONGS PA DANG, RNYED PA DANG, BKUR STI
DANG, TSIGS SU BCAD PA DANG, THEG PA DMAN PA DANG, SKYE BO MI
BGRUNGS PA DANG MA 'DRES PA'O, ,SEMS BSKYED PA BLA NA MED PA BZHI
NI PHANGS PA THAMS CAD GTONG BA DANG, BTANG NAS MI 'GYOD PA DANG,

RNAM PAR SMIN PA LA MI RE BA DANG, BYANG CHUB TU BSNGO BA'I SEMS
BYA'O, ,SPYI BOR PHYIN PA'I CHOS BZHI NI, SHES RAB KYI PHA ROL DU
PHYIN PA DANG, THABS LA MKHAS PA DANG, DAM PA'I CHOS 'DZIN PA
DANG, SEMS CAN SMIN PAR BYED PA'O, ,CHOS GYA NOM PA DANG, DAM
PA'I MCHOG

BZHI NI SEMS CAN LA KHONG KHRO BA MED PA DANG, GANG DAG 'GAL BAR
BYED PA DAG NYID LA RAB TU THAR BAR BYA BAR SEMS BSKYED PA DANG,
YUL RGYA CHEN PO 'BYOR KYANG DE LA BAG YOD PA DANG, DBUL BAS
PHONGS KYANG CHOS SPYOD PA'O, ,DGE BA'I CHOS BZHI NI, DGE BA
THAMS CAD LA SBYOR BA

PA'O, ,TSANGS PAS BYIN GYIS ZHUS PA LAS, CHOS BZHI DANG LDAN NA
BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' DMU RGOD YIN TE, GANG ZHE NA, KHVA LTAR

@325A *, ,GTONG NGO, ,SKYED PAR BYED PA'I BDAG NYID RGYU'I RGYUN

BYON PA LHUNG BZED CHAG PA, SHES BZHIN MED PA, SPYOD LAM MI SDUG

KYIS BTAB BA 'BYUNG BAR 'GYUR RO, ,CI'I PHYIR ZHE NA, DE'I TSE
DGE SLONG DAG

PHAL CHER BSNYEN BKUR DANG RNYED PA DANG, BKUR STI 'DOD PA BYA BA
